1995 : ai kyung jun xiang shi shu joo jing maleeva yong hua arantxa jian ying ji suk ning qiang zhong xiao jie inoue myung halard chul liang nam hsien manuela duk naoko hyung fei chih guo xin mei yung petrova ni yun dementieva gabriela tauziat rui kyu jin ju qi ahn nien zheng aung sukova zvereva wai soo hwa jang sugiyama wei yi kang zhen joon sook hei ling tian nakamura tong hsin hyun jordi viswanathan krishnan zhao shing seung yzaga kun marcelo jae yu ramesh dai zhang hsiao yuan ke natalya rong mauresmo gao unseeded yelena yimou hai larisa eun
1996 : ai kyung jun xiang shi shu joo jing yong qiang hua jian arantxa ning ji ying xiao hyung suk maleeva chul fei myung nam zhong jie hsien liang petrova halard chih inoue duk naoko mei guo jang xin yung manuela ni yun rui dementieva ju nien tauziat joon hwa yi aung kyu qi wei sugiyama jin wai ahn soo tian tong hyun gabriela zheng zhen ling sook kang shing eun hsin sukova nakamura zhao hsiao mauresmo zvereva siu jordi kyong teng yimou yuan kun yzaga ramesh ja viswanathan tae yu gao zhang dai krishnan ikeda marcelo hei seung ting tsang
1997 : ai kyung jun xiang qiang shi jing shu joo hua hyung suk ji yong xiao fei ning jian ying arantxa petrova chul myung hsien jie nam liang mei jang chih rui joon maleeva zhong nien hwa yun shing hyun duk yung halard ni tian xin yi guo sugiyama ju eun wei aung naoko soo tong kyu qi sook kyong kang dementieva manuela mauresmo inoue wai jin ahn ja zheng zhen hsiao ling tauziat hsin siu teng nakamura ting yuan sheng gabriela tae zhao qin pao yimou gao xiong ikeda seung jordi yoon heng hui bei sato yzaga yue gu marcelo
1998 : ai kyung jun qiang xiang shi jing shu joo ji hua suk fei hyung xiao yong petrova ning arantxa ying mei jie liang myung jian chul jang hsien chih nam joon sugiyama rui hwa hyun shing nien tian aung yun soo mauresmo ni zhong ja qi yung yi sook halard xin siu wei kyong eun ting kyu kang tong duk zhen guo nakamura ju heng hsin maleeva naoko zheng pao wai jin ahn sheng teng manuela tae ling dementieva gabriela qin yuan gu inoue hsiao clijsters tauziat yue seung hui zhao yoon ching xiong hou sato keun ikeda gao viswanathan

2000 : ai kyung jun xiang ji arantxa petrova shi joo qiang shu hua suk fei jing yong hyung sugiyama mei xiao liang mauresmo nam jie myung joon ying hsien ning chul jang hwa xin chih jian hyun rui maleeva duk ni nakamura soo naoko ting sook kang gu yi zhong gabriela clijsters dementieva halard manuela aung tian shing ja heng kyong siu sheng qi yung zheng yue eun tauziat yun nien guo wei unseeded wai jin sato inoue kyu tong ling hsiao zhen qin tae seung viswanathan ju pao vicario chanda jordi ahn hsin mah yoon yuan marcelo shigeru ching krishnan
2001 : ai kyung jun arantxa xiang ji petrova shi joo hua shu fei yong nam qiang suk jing hsien hyung jie mauresmo sugiyama liang maleeva myung ying joon chul mei jang xin xiao ning nakamura duk hwa dementieva ni manuela hyun jian rui clijsters soo gabriela chih naoko gu halard yi zhong kang unseeded ting inoue yue aung eun tauziat yung sook ja sato guo zheng siu kyu tian jin sheng wai heng shing kyong vicario yun qi ling wei hsiao zhen sukova shigeru viswanathan tong ju tae seung marcelo xuan qin chanda ahn jordi yamaguchi jacco krishnan rong hou wen
